\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04783}04783   \textcolor{comment}{// calculate  F2\_12 = f2\_12 -\/ f1\_1*f1\_2  and R2 = f2/f1\_1/f1\_2 -\/ 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04784}04784   \textcolor{comment}{// errors are calculated assuming there are no correlations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04785}04785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04786}04786   \textcolor{keywordtype}{double} ref1\_1, ref1\_2, ref2\_12;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04787}04787   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (f1\_1<1E-\/20 || f1\_2<1E-\/20)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04788}04788     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04789}04789     F2\_12  = 0.0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04791}04791     R2\_12  = 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04792}04792     eR2\_12 = 0.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04793}04793     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04794}04794   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04795}04795     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04796}04796     F2\_12     = f2\_12 -\/ f1\_1*f1\_2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04797}04797     ref1\_1    = ef1\_1/f1\_1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_histogram_collection_8cpp_source_l04798}04798     ref1\_2    = ef1\_2/f1\_2;}
